// I-cd-031 (#621): demo journey end-to-end — home → template → ask
// (intake) → run-step (dashboard) → inspector → claim-source.
//
// Verifies each step's landing page renders + links forward to the next
// step. The "run" step itself is hardware-bound (real pipeline-A), so the
// test pivots at /dashboard to /inspector/v1-canonical-success — the
// frozen I-A-02b fixture (I-cd-012) that the gold-route Inspector
// renders. That step's assertions cover the verified-report → claim →
// source provenance UI surface.

import { expect, test } from "@playwright/test";

test("demo journey: home → intake → dashboard → inspector (canonical fixture)", async ({
  page,
}) => {
  // Step 1: home renders + clinical template card present + linked.
  await page.goto("/");
  await expect(page.getByTestId("template-card-clinical")).toBeVisible();
  await expect(page.getByTestId("template-card-clinical-link")).toBeVisible();
  const intake_link = page.getByTestId("template-card-clinical-link").first();
  await intake_link.click();

  // Step 2: lands on /intake?template=clinical with the intake form.
  await expect(page).toHaveURL(/\/intake\?template=clinical/);
  await expect(page.getByTestId("intake-page")).toBeVisible();

  // Step 3: dashboard is reachable directly (the "ask a question" UX
  // entry). The intake page funnels here for clinical questions.
  await page.goto("/dashboard");
  await expect(page.getByTestId("dashboard-page")).toBeVisible();

  // Step 4: inspector renders the canonical v1.0 fixture (I-A-02b
  // frozen schema, the contract Carney's office reviews).
  await page.goto("/inspector/v1-canonical-success");
  await expect(page.getByTestId("inspector-view")).toBeVisible({
    timeout: 10_000,
  });

  // Step 5: claim → source UI surface — the family-segregation badge
  // proves the two-family invariant (CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 1)
  // surfaces to the reviewer.
  await expect(page.getByTestId("inspector-view")).toContainText(
    /generator|evaluator|two-family/i,
  );
});

test("demo journey nav-parity: header + primary nav identical across journey routes", async ({
  page,
}) => {
  for (const path of [
    "/",
    "/intake",

+// I-cd-031 (#621): demo journey end-to-end — home → template → ask
+// (intake) → run-step (dashboard) → inspector → claim-source.
+//
+// Verifies each step's landing page renders + links forward to the next
+// step. The "run" step itself is hardware-bound (real pipeline-A), so the
+// test pivots at /dashboard to /inspector/v1-canonical-success — the
+// frozen I-A-02b fixture (I-cd-012) that the gold-route Inspector
+// renders. That step's assertions cover the verified-report → claim →
+// source provenance UI surface.
+
+import { expect, test } from "@playwright/test";
+
+test("demo journey: home → intake → dashboard → inspector (canonical fixture)", async ({
+  page,
+}) => {
+  // Step 1: home renders + clinical template card present + linked.
+  await page.goto("/");
+  await expect(page.getByTestId("template-card-clinical")).toBeVisible();
+  await expect(page.getByTestId("template-card-clinical-link")).toBeVisible();
+  const intake_link = page.getByTestId("template-card-clinical-link").first();
+  await intake_link.click();
+
+  // Step 2: lands on /intake?template=clinical with the intake form.
+  await expect(page).toHaveURL(/\/intake\?template=clinical/);
+  await expect(page.getByTestId("intake-page")).toBeVisible();
+
+  // Step 3: dashboard is reachable directly (the "ask a question" UX
+  // entry). The intake page funnels here for clinical questions.
+  await page.goto("/dashboard");
+  await expect(page.getByTestId("dashboard-page")).toBeVisible();
+
+  // Step 4: inspector renders the canonical v1.0 fixture (I-A-02b
+  // frozen schema, the contract Carney's office reviews).
+  await page.goto("/inspector/v1-canonical-success");
+  await expect(page.getByTestId("inspector-view")).toBeVisible({
+    timeout: 10_000,
+  });
+
+  // Step 5: claim → source UI surface — the family-segregation badge
+  // proves the two-family invariant (CLAUDE.md §9.1 invariant 1)
+  // surfaces to the reviewer.
+  await expect(page.getByTestId("inspector-view")).toContainText(
+    /generator|evaluator|two-family/i,
+  );
+});
+
+test("demo journey nav-parity: header + primary nav identical across journey routes", async ({
+  page,
+}) => {
+  for (const path of [
+    "/",
+    "/intake",
+    "/dashboard",
+    "/inspector/v1-canonical-success",
+  ]) {
+    await page.goto(path);
+    await expect(page.locator("header")).toHaveCount(1);
+    const nav = page.locator("nav[aria-label='Primary']");
+    await expect(nav).toBeVisible();
+    for (const label of [
+      "Home",
+      "Intake",
+      "Dashboard",
+      "Inspector".replace("Inspector", "Upload"), // Inspector isn't in primary nav
+    ]) {
+      if (label === "Upload") {
+        await expect(nav.getByRole("link", { name: label })).toBeVisible();
+      }
+    }
+  }
+});

defaults:
  run:
    working-directory: web

jobs:
  lint_format_typecheck_build:
    name: lint + format + typecheck + build
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - name: checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: setup_node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: "22"
          cache: "npm"
          cache-dependency-path: web/package-lock.json

      - name: install_dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: lint
        run: npm run lint

      - name: format_check
        run: npm run format:check

      - name: typecheck
        run: npm run typecheck

      - name: build
        run: npm run build

  e2e_playwright:
    name: e2e + a11y + perf (Playwright on Chromium)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint_format_typecheck_build
    steps:
      - name: checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: setup_node
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: "22"
          cache: "npm"
          cache-dependency-path: web/package-lock.json

      - name: setup_python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.13"
          cache: "pip"

      - name: install_python_dependencies
        working-directory: ${{ github.workspace }}
        run: |
          python -m pip install --upgrade pip
          pip install -r requirements.txt

      - name: install_npm_dependencies
        run: npm ci

      - name: install_playwright_chromium
        run: npx playwright install --with-deps chromium

      - name: start_fastapi_backend
        working-directory: ${{ github.workspace }}
        run: |
          PYTHONPATH=src nohup python -m uvicorn polaris_v6.api.app:app \
            --host 127.0.0.1 --port 8000 \
            > /tmp/fastapi.log 2>&1 &
          # Wait for /health to respond.
          for i in {1..30}; do
            if curl -fs http://127.0.0.1:8000/health > /dev/null; then
              echo "backend ready"
              exit 0
            fi
            sleep 1
          done
          echo "backend failed to start"
          cat /tmp/fastapi.log
          exit 1

      - name: build_and_start_next
        # I-cd-015 (GH#611): POLARIS_TEST_HARNESS_ENABLED=1 lets the prod
        # build serve harness routes for tests that depend on them
        # (evidence_tooltip_perf etc.). Real production leaves this UNSET
        # and the middleware 404s /charts_test/*, /sentence_hover_test/*,
        # /disambiguation_modal_preview/*, /generation/*, /retrieval/*, /sse/*.
        env:
          POLARIS_TEST_HARNESS_ENABLED: "1"
        run: |
          npm run build
          nohup npx next start -p 3738 > /tmp/next.log 2>&1 &
          # Wait for /dashboard to respond.
          for i in {1..30}; do
            if curl -fs http://127.0.0.1:3738/dashboard > /dev/null; then
              echo "frontend ready"
              exit 0
            fi
            sleep 1
          done
          echo "frontend failed to start"
          cat /tmp/next.log
          exit 1

  verify_pip_resolution:
    # F-22 (cycle-7 P1.1 prevention): catches pip dependency conflicts
    # before they reach pytest_v6_backend or the production Dockerfile.
    # Cycle-7 caught F-17's protobuf>=6.33.5 pin breaking against
    # google-generativeai's transitive protobuf<5.0.0 constraint.
    name: pip install --dry-run (catch ResolutionImpossible early)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: lint_format_typecheck_build
    steps:
      - name: checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: setup_python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.13"

      - name: pip_dry_run_legacy_requirements
        # If this fails, requirements.txt has a conflict; production
        # Dockerfile build would fail in the same way.
        run: pip install --dry-run -r requirements.txt

      - name: pip_dry_run_v6_requirements
        # Verify the v6 backend's pinned set also resolves cleanly.
        run: pip install --dry-run -r requirements-v6.txt

  pytest_v6_backend:
    name: pytest tests/v6/ (Phase 0 backend coverage)
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: [lint_format_typecheck_build, verify_pip_resolution]
    defaults:
      run:
        working-directory: ${{ github.workspace }}
    steps:
      - name: checkout
        uses: actions/checkout@v4

      - name: setup_python
        uses: actions/setup-python@v5
        with:
          python-version: "3.13"
          cache: "pip"

      # Cycle-3 audit P2.3 (outputs/audits/continuous/bb60495_audit.md):
      # tests/v6/test_*_middleware.py + test_actors.py + test_broker.py +
      # test_otel_init.py use pytest.importorskip against dramatiq +
      # opentelemetry deps. Without -v6.txt installed they SILENTLY SKIP
      # (LAW II violation). This job uses requirements-v6.txt as the
      # canonical pin source for v6 backend code.
      - name: install_v6_dependencies
        run: |
          python -m pip install --upgrade pip
          pip install -r requirements-v6.txt

      - name: run_pytest_v6
        env:
          PYTHONPATH: src
        # `-q` keeps output tight; `--strict-markers` fails on undefined
        # markers; `--no-header` removes pytest banner from CI logs.
        # Acceptance suite (tests/v6/acceptance/) is excluded — it requires
        # a live broker; covered by tests/v6/acceptance/test_dramatiq_acceptance.py
        # which runs in its own integration job once Vast.ai cluster is live.
        run: |
          pytest tests/v6/ \
            --ignore=tests/v6/acceptance \
            -q --strict-markers --no-header

  37: export function HomeKeyboardShell({ templates, signInHref, children }: Props) {
  38:   const [palette_open, set_palette_open] = useState(false);
  39:   const sign_in_link_ref = useRef<HTMLAnchorElement>(null);
  40: 
  41:   useEffect(() => {
  42:     function on_keydown(event: KeyboardEvent) {
  43:       if ((event.metaKey || event.ctrlKey) && event.key === "k") {
  44:         event.preventDefault();
  45:         event.stopPropagation();
  46:         set_palette_open((p) => !p);
  47:       }
  48:     }
  49:     window.addEventListener("keydown", on_keydown);
  50:     return () => window.removeEventListener("keydown", on_keydown);
  51:   }, []);
  52: 
  53:   return (
  54:     <>
  55:       <header className="border-border bg-background border-b">
  56:         <div className="mx-auto flex w-full max-w-7xl items-center justify-between gap-6 px-6 py-3">
  57:           <Link
  58:             href="/"
  59:             className="text-foreground font-mono text-sm font-semibold tracking-tight"
  60:           >
  61:             POLARIS · Canada
  62:           </Link>
  63:           <nav className="flex items-center gap-1" aria-label="Primary">
  64:             {PRIMARY_NAV.map((item) => (
  65:               <NavLink key={item.href} href={item.href}>
  66:                 {item.label}
  67:               </NavLink>
  68:             ))}
  69:           </nav>
  70:           <Button
  71:             variant="outline"
  72:             nativeButton={false}
  73:             render={
  74:               <Link
  75:                 ref={sign_in_link_ref}
  76:                 data-testid="header-sign-in-link"
  77:                 href={signInHref}
  78:               />
  79:             }
  80:           >
  81:             Sign in
  82:           </Button>
  83:         </div>
  84:       </header>
  85:       {children}
  86:       <CommandPalette
  87:         open={palette_open}
  88:         onOpenChange={set_palette_open}
  89:         templates={templates}
  90:         signInLinkRef={sign_in_link_ref}
  91:       />
  92:     </>
  93:   );
  94: }

   7: // can still wrap every non-home route on the server.
   8: "use client";
   9: 
  10: import { usePathname } from "next/navigation";
  11: 
  12: import { AppShell } from "@/components/app_shell";
  13: 
  14: interface AppShellGateProps {
  15:   children: React.ReactNode;
  16: }
  17: 
  18: export function AppShellGate({ children }: AppShellGateProps) {
  19:   const pathname = usePathname();
  20:   // Home owns its own header + main; render children bare on `/`.

   1: """I-carney-004 — static-accounts auth + HS256 JWT.
   2: 
   3: Pattern (Carney-demo scope):
   4: - Operator-curated YAML at `${POLARIS_STATIC_ACCOUNTS_PATH:-/app/config/static_accounts.yaml}`
   5:   with bcrypt-hashed passwords + role.
   6: - POST /auth/login → 12-hour HS256 JWT signed with POLARIS_JWT_SECRET.
   7: - `require_auth` FastAPI dependency injects on all routes except an allowlist
   8:   (/health, /transparency*, /auth/login).
   9: 
  10: LAW II: missing POLARIS_JWT_SECRET at app startup → fail-loud RuntimeError.
  11: Never silently allow unauthenticated traffic.
  12: 
  13: Phase-2: replace with Cognito/Okta when the demo gives way to long-term use.
  14: """
  15: 
  16: from __future__ import annotations
  17: 
  18: import os
  19: import secrets
  20: from datetime import datetime, timedelta, timezone
  21: from pathlib import Path
  22: from typing import Any
  23: 
  24: import yaml
  25: from fastapi import APIRouter, Depends, HTTPException, Request
  26: from fastapi.security import HTTPAuthorizationCredentials, HTTPBearer
  27: from jose import JWTError, jwt
  28: from passlib.context import CryptContext
  29: from pydantic import BaseModel
  30: 
  31: JWT_ALGORITHM = "HS256"
  32: JWT_EXPIRY_HOURS = 12
  33: 
  34: # Paths exempt from auth — health probes + reviewer-visible transparency.
  35: PUBLIC_PATH_PREFIXES: tuple[str, ...] = (
  36:     "/health",
  37:     "/transparency",
  38:     "/auth/login",
  39:     "/docs",       # FastAPI's own OpenAPI UI
  40:     "/redoc",
  41:     "/openapi.json",
  42: )
  43: 
  44: DEFAULT_ACCOUNTS_PATH = "/app/config/static_accounts.yaml"
  45: 
  46: _pwd_ctx = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")
  47: _bearer_scheme = HTTPBearer(auto_error=False)
  48: router = APIRouter(tags=["auth"])
  49: 
  50: 
  51: class LoginRequest(BaseModel):
  52:     username: str
  53:     password: str
  54: 
  55: 
  56: class LoginResponse(BaseModel):
  57:     access_token: str
  58:     token_type: str = "bearer"
  59:     role: str
  60:     expires_in: int  # seconds
  61: 
  62: 
  63: class User(BaseModel):
  64:     username: str
  65:     role: str
  66: 
  67: 
  68: def _load_accounts() -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
  69:     """Read the static-accounts YAML. Raises RuntimeError if missing.
  70: 
  71:     LAW II: never silently default to an empty account list (which would
  72:     behave as 'allow nobody' but the operator would not realize the file
  73:     was missing).
  74:     """
  75:     path = Path(os.environ.get("POLARIS_STATIC_ACCOUNTS_PATH", DEFAULT_ACCOUNTS_PATH))
  76:     if not path.exists():
  77:         raise RuntimeError(
  78:             f"static_accounts.yaml not found at {path}. Set "
  79:             "POLARIS_STATIC_ACCOUNTS_PATH or mount the file. The application "
  80:             "refuses to start without the auth substrate (LAW II)."
  81:         )
  82:     body = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
  83:     if not isinstance(body, dict) or not isinstance(body.get("accounts"), list):
  84:         raise RuntimeError(f"static_accounts.yaml at {path} must have top-level 'accounts' list")
  85:     return body["accounts"]
  86: 
  87: 
  88: def _jwt_secret() -> str:
  89:     secret = os.environ.get("POLARIS_JWT_SECRET", "").strip()
  90:     if not secret or len(secret) < 32:
  91:         raise RuntimeError(
  92:             "POLARIS_JWT_SECRET env var missing or too short (<32 chars). "
  93:             "Application refuses to issue tokens with a weak/missing key (LAW II). "
  94:             "Set via AWS Secrets Manager → cloud-init → .env per I-carney-004."
  95:         )
  96:     return secret
  97: 
  98: 
  99: def verify_app_startup() -> None:
 100:     """Called at FastAPI app create_app() time. Fail loud if auth substrate
 101:     is misconfigured. Per LAW II, we never start an auth-gated app with a
 102:     broken auth gate.
 103: 
 104:     Skipped when POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED=1 (Phase-0 demo + tests).
 105:     """
 106:     if os.environ.get("POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED", "") == "1":
 107:         return
 108:     _jwt_secret()
 109:     _load_accounts()  # raises if YAML missing or malformed
 110: 
 111: 
 112: def issue_token(username: str, role: str) -> tuple[str, int]:
 113:     """Returns (jwt, expires_in_seconds)."""
 114:     expires_in = JWT_EXPIRY_HOURS * 3600
 115:     payload = {
 116:         "sub": username,
 117:         "role": role,
 118:         "iat": datetime.now(timezone.utc),
 119:         "exp": datetime.now(timezone.utc) + timedelta(hours=JWT_EXPIRY_HOURS),
 120:     }
 121:     token = jwt.encode(payload, _jwt_secret(), algorithm=JWT_ALGORITHM)
 122:     return token, expires_in
 123: 
 124: 
 125: def _path_is_public(path: str) -> bool:
 126:     return any(path.startswith(prefix) for prefix in PUBLIC_PATH_PREFIXES)
 127: 
 128: 
 129: async def require_auth(
 130:     request: Request,
 131:     creds: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials | None = Depends(_bearer_scheme),
 132: ) -> User | None:
 133:     """Global FastAPI dependency. None on public paths; raises 401 otherwise.
 134: 
 135:     Phase-0 demo: POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED=1 short-circuits to None (auth off).
 136:     """
 137:     if os.environ.get("POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED", "") == "1":
 138:         return None
 139:     if _path_is_public(request.url.path):
 140:         return None
